class="h-display-body" data-reactid="2574">VeeR and Mararché du film has been partnering to run Cannes XR for the third year in a row. VeeR coordinates the entire festival from project collection, jury invitation to the online showcase and the final ceremony where the Best VR Story Award and the Best Interactive Experience Award will be awarded. VeeR is also bringing the festival offline to increase visibility and exposure around the world.</div><br data-reactid="2575"><div class="h-display-body margin-b-m" data-reactid="2576"></div><div class="margin-b-m cannes__link" data-reactid="2577"><a href="https://www.marchedufilm.com/programs/cannes-xr/veer-future-award/" data-reactid="2578">Cannes XR official website</a><a href="https://www.marchedufilm.com/programs/cannes-xr/veer-future-award/veer-future-award-projects/" data-reactid="2579">2022 Cannes XR project shortlist</a></div></div></div><div class="cannes__box margin-b-m" data-reactid="2580"><div class="box w-12-4" data-reactid="2581"><div class="h-body margin-b-16 " data-reactid="2582">VR introduced me to a new dimension of visual presentation. I believe this technology allows the creators to explore different ways of story telling, and gives them more room to express their ideas. I hope to see more VR integration in traditional film and TV content, so the audience can have a brand new experience.</div><div class="h-body text-right" data-reactid="2583">—— Changwei Gu</div><div class="h-body text-right" data-reactid="2584">Head of Jury of 2021 Cannes XR, internationally renowned film director </div></div><div class="box w-12-4" data-reactid="2585"><div class="h-body margin-b-16 " data-reactid="2586">VeeR has been an important and reliable partner of Marché du film and Cannes XR..... I hope to see more VR integration in traditional film and TV content, so the audience can have a brand new experience.</div><div class="h-body text-right" data-reactid="3036">—— Changwei Gu</div><div class="h-body text-right" data-reactid="3037">Head of Jury of 2021 Cannes XR, internationally renowned film director </div></div><div class="box margin-b-16" data-reactid="3038"><div class="h-body margin-b-16" data-reactid="3039">VeeR has been an important and reliable partner of Marché du film and Cannes XR.....
